01; A convention of this file is that lines starting with semicolon are comments
; Begun approx. Apr 2016
; Each line is represented in two forms:
;  F  is the final sandhi form; this is the version one sees printed
;  A  is the analyzed sandhi form.  Here words are separated, if needed,
;     and word endings are changed to their original (pre-sandhi) form.
;     This step of analysis facilitates the further analysis of grammatical
;     form
; There is sometimes an additional form, as it appears in the source of
; this digitization.  Namely, compound-analysis. See 0047 as example.
; 
0044F: .. hitopadeSaH ..
0044A: .. hitopadeSaH ..

;0045F:        maNgalAcaraRam
; Kale has 'prastAvikA'
0045F: prastAvikA      
0045A: prastAvikA
